(pr1 p ▹ id₁ (pr1 disp_map_slice_bifinal_obj))
• runitor (pr1 β) =
(pr1 q ▹ id₁ (pr1 disp_map_slice_bifinal_obj))
• runitor (pr1 β)

b: B

pr1 q ▹ id₁ (pr1 disp_map_slice_bifinal_obj)

b: B

disp_map_slice_bifinal_obj ⟧
p, q: α ==> β
pr122 α
• (pr1 p ▹ id₁ (pr1 disp_map_slice_bifinal_obj)) =
pr122 α
• (pr1 q ▹ id₁ (pr1 disp_map_slice_bifinal_obj))

    exact (pr2 p @ !(pr2 q)).
  Qed.

(**
 2. Products
 *)
Section DisplayMapBicatProduct.
  Context {B : bicat}
          (D : disp_map_bicat B)
          (D_comp : arrow_subbicat_closed_composition D)
          (D_mor : arrow_subbicat_closed_prod_mor D)
          {pb x y b : B}
          {f : x --> b}
          (Hf : pred_ob D f)
          {g : y --> b}
          (Hg : pred_ob D g)
          (π₁ : pb --> x)
          (π₂ : pb --> y)
          (γ : invertible_2cell (π₁ · f) (π₂ · g))
          (cone : pb_cone f g := make_pb_cone _ π₁ π₂ γ)
          (Hpb : has_pb_ump cone).

  Let ff : disp_map_slice_bicat D b
    := x ,, f ,, Hf.
  Let gg : disp_map_slice_bicat D b
    := y ,, g ,, Hg.

  
B: bicat
D: disp_map_bicat B
D_comp: arrow_subbicat_closed_composition D
D_mor: arrow_subbicat_closed_prod_mor D
pb, x, y, b: B
f: B ⟦ x, b ⟧
Hf: pred_ob D f
g: B ⟦ y, b ⟧
Hg: pred_ob D g
π₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
π₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (π₁ · f) (π₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb π₁ π₂ γ: pb_cone f g
Hpb: has_pb_ump cone
ff:= x,, f,, Hf: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
gg:= y,, g,, Hg: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
binprod_cone ff gg

  (comp_of_invertible_2cell
     (pr22 (binprod_cone_pr1 q))
     (rwhisker_of_invertible_2cell 
        (pr12 ff)
        (inv_of_invertible_2cell
           (pb_ump_mor_pr1 Hpb other_cone))))
  (rassociator_invertible_2cell
     (pb_ump_mor Hpb other_cone) 
     (pb_cone_pr1 cone) 
     (pr12 ff)): invertible_2cell (pr121 q)
  (pb_ump_mor Hpb other_cone · (π₁ · f))
pr22 (binprod_cone_pr1 q)
• (((pb_ump_mor_pr1 Hpb other_cone) ^-1 ▹ f)
   • (rassociator (pb_ump_mor Hpb other_cone) π₁ f
      • (lassociator (pr1 Hpb other_cone) π₁ f
         • ((pb_1cell_pr1 (pr1 Hpb other_cone) ▹ f)
            • ((pr22 (binprod_cone_pr1 q)) ^-1
               • (pr22 (binprod_cone_pr2 q)
                  • (((pb_1cell_pr2
                         (pr1 Hpb other_cone)) ^-1 ▹ g)
                     • (rassociator
                          (pr1 Hpb other_cone) π₂ g
                        • (lassociator
                             (pb_ump_mor Hpb
                                other_cone) π₂ g
                           • (pb_ump_mor_pr2 Hpb
                                other_cone ▹ g)))))))))) =
pr122 (binprod_cone_pr2 q)

π₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (π₁ · f) (π₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb π₁ π₂ γ: pb_cone f g
Hpb: has_pb_ump cone
ff:= x,, f,, Hf: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
gg:= y,, g,, Hg: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
q: binprod_cone ff gg
other_cone:= make_pb_cone (pr1 q)
  (pr1 (binprod_cone_pr1 q))
  (pr1 (binprod_cone_pr2 q))
  (comp_of_invertible_2cell
     (inv_of_invertible_2cell
        (pr22 (binprod_cone_pr1 q)))
     (pr22 (binprod_cone_pr2 q))): pb_cone f g
φ:= comp_of_invertible_2cell
  (comp_of_invertible_2cell
     (pr22 (binprod_cone_pr1 q))
     (rwhisker_of_invertible_2cell 
        (pr12 ff)
        (inv_of_invertible_2cell
           (pb_ump_mor_pr1 Hpb other_cone))))
  (rassociator_invertible_2cell
     (pb_ump_mor Hpb other_cone) 
     (pb_cone_pr1 cone) 
     (pr12 ff)): invertible_2cell (pr121 q)
  (pb_ump_mor Hpb other_cone · (π₁ · f))
((((id₂ (pr12 q) • pr22 (binprod_cone_pr2 q))
   • ((pb_1cell_pr2 (pr1 Hpb other_cone)) ^-1 ▹ g))
  • rassociator (pr1 Hpb other_cone) π₂ g)
 • lassociator (pb_ump_mor Hpb other_cone) π₂ g)
• (pb_ump_mor_pr2 Hpb other_cone ▹ g) =
pr122 (binprod_cone_pr2 q)

   ▹ binprod_cone_pr1 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice =
   α
   × x0
     ▹ binprod_cone_pr2 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice =
     β)

        apply isapropdirprod ; apply cellset_property.

▹ binprod_cone_pr1 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice =

× χ
  ▹ binprod_cone_pr2
      binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice = β
r₁:= pr2 α: (λ η : pr1
         (φ
          · binprod_cone_pr1
              binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice) ==>
       pr1
         (ψ
          · binprod_cone_pr1
              binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice),
 disp_2cells η
   (pr2
      (φ
       · binprod_cone_pr1
           binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice))
   (pr2
      (ψ
       · binprod_cone_pr1
           binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice)))
  (pr1 α)
(((pr1 φ ◃ γ) • lassociator (pr1 φ) π₂ g)
 • (pr1 β ▹ g)) • rassociator (pr1 ψ) π₂ g =
((lassociator (pr1 φ) π₁ f • (pr1 α ▹ f))
 • rassociator (pr1 ψ) π₁ f) • (pr1 ψ ◃ γ)

• (lassociator (pr1 ψ) π₁ f
   • (rassociator (pr1 ψ) π₁ f • (pr1 ψ ◃ γ)))

B: bicat
D: disp_map_bicat B
D_comp: arrow_subbicat_closed_composition D
D_mor: arrow_subbicat_closed_prod_mor D
pb, x, y, b: B
f: B ⟦ x, b ⟧
Hf: pred_ob D f
g: B ⟦ y, b ⟧
Hg: pred_ob D g
π₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
π₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (π₁ · f) (π₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb π₁ π₂ γ: pb_cone f g
Hpb: has_pb_ump cone
ff:= x,, f,, Hf: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
gg:= y,, g,, Hg: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
h: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
φ, ψ: disp_map_slice_bicat D b ⟦ h,
binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice ⟧
α: φ
· binprod_cone_pr1 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice ==>
ψ
· binprod_cone_pr1 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice
β: φ
· binprod_cone_pr2 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice ==>
ψ
· binprod_cone_pr2 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice
(((pr1 φ ◃ γ) • lassociator (pr1 φ) π₂ g)
 • (pr1 β ▹ g)) • rassociator (pr1 ψ) π₂ g =
((lassociator (pr1 φ) π₁ f • (pr1 α ▹ f))
 • rassociator (pr1 ψ) π₁ f) • (pr1 ψ ◃ γ)

        abstract
          (pose (r₁ := pr2 α) ;
           pose (r₂ := pr2 β) ;
           cbn in r₁, r₂ ;
           rewrite !lwhisker_id2, !id2_left in r₁ ;
           use (vcomp_lcancel (pr22 φ)) ; [ apply property_from_invertible_2cell | ] ;
           rewrite !vassocr ;
           rewrite !vassocr in r₂ ;
           refine (maponpaths (λ z, z • _) r₂ @ _) ; clear r₂ ;
           refine (_ @ maponpaths (λ z, (z • _) • _) (!r₁)) ; clear r₁ ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           apply maponpaths ;
           rewrite lassociator_rassociator, id2_right ;
           rewrite !vassocr ;
           rewrite lassociator_rassociator, id2_left ;
           apply idpath).
      
B: bicat
D: disp_map_bicat B
D_comp: arrow_subbicat_closed_composition D
D_mor: arrow_subbicat_closed_prod_mor D
pb, x, y, b: B
f: B ⟦ x, b ⟧
Hf: pred_ob D f
g: B ⟦ y, b ⟧
Hg: pred_ob D g
π₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
π₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (π₁ · f) (π₂ · g)
cone:= make_pb_cone pb π₁ π₂ γ: pb_cone f g
Hpb: has_pb_ump cone
ff:= x,, f,, Hf: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
gg:= y,, g,, Hg: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
h: disp_map_slice_bicat D b
φ, ψ: disp_map_slice_bicat D b ⟦ h,
binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice ⟧
α: φ
· binprod_cone_pr1 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice ==>
ψ
· binprod_cone_pr1 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice
β: φ
· binprod_cone_pr2 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice ==>
ψ
· binprod_cone_pr2 binprod_cone_in_disp_map_slice
(λ η : pr1 φ ==> pr1 ψ, disp_2cells η (pr2 φ) (pr2 ψ))
  (pb_ump_cell Hpb (pr1 φ) (pr1 ψ) (pr1 α) (pr1 β)
     (binprod_2_ump_in_disp_map_slice_cell_subproof
      :
      (((pr1 φ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)
        • lassociator (pr1 φ) (pb_cone_pr2 cone) g)
       • (pr1 β ▹ g))
      • rassociator (pr1 ψ) (pb_cone_pr2 cone) g =
      ((lassociator (pr1 φ) (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f
        • (pr1 α ▹ f))
       • rassociator (pr1 ψ) (pb_cone_pr1 cone) f)
      • (pr1 ψ ◃ pb_cone_cell cone)))
 abstract
          (cbn ;
           use (vcomp_rcancel (lassociator _ _ _)) ; [ is_iso | ] ;
           rewrite !vassocl ;
           rewrite <- rwhisker_rwhisker ;
           rewrite (pb_ump_cell_pr1 Hpb) ;
           pose (pr2 α) as r ;
           cbn in r ;
           rewrite !lwhisker_id2, !id2_left in r ;
           rewrite !vassocr ;
           exact r).
    Defined.

    
B: bicat
D: disp_map_bicat B
D_comp: arrow_subbicat_closed_composition D
D_mor: arrow_subbicat_closed_prod_mor D
pb, x, y, b: B
f: B ⟦ x, b ⟧
Hf: pred_ob D f
g: B ⟦ y, b ⟧
Hg: pred_ob D g
π₁: B ⟦ pb, x ⟧
π₂: B ⟦ pb, y ⟧
γ: invertible_2cell (π₁ · f) (π₂ · g)
